   // context for modal template
var modalContext = {
	'class': 'Modal--fullSmallOnly Modal--fullMediumSmallOnly',
	'id': 'intro-video-modal',
	'header': {
		'text': '<h2 class=\"u-margin-none\">Introduction to eBird<\/h2>'
	},
	'content': {
		'text': '<div class=\"Panel u-padding-none\"><iframe id=\"intro-video\" width=\"720\" height=\"405\" src=\"https:\/\/www.youtube.com\/embed\/-t-0xAjxakw?enablejsapi=1&modestbranding=1&rel=0&showinfo=0&autoplay=1\" style=\"max-width:100%;\" frameborder=\"0\" gesture=\"media\" allow=\"encrypted-media\" allowfullscreen autoplay><\/iframe><\/div><div class=\"Blurb Blurb--centered\"><div class=\"Blurb-link\">\t<a href=\"https://secure.birds.cornell.edu/cassso/account/create?service=https://ebird.org/login/cas?portal=ebird\" class=\"Button Button--highlight\">Get started<\/a><\/div><\/div>'
	},
	'footer': false
};

$(function() {
	$('#intro-video-play').click(function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();

		// render the templates
		var modal = Handlebars.templates.Modal(modalContext);
		$('body')
			.append('<div class="Modal-background" data-modal-background=""></div>')
			.append(modal);

		// focus on something in the modal (iframe? anchor?)
		$('[data-panel=Modal][aria-hidden=false] button').focus();

		// handle closing modal
		$(document).on('modal:hide', function() {
			$('[data-modal-background]').remove();
			$('#intro-video-modal').remove();
		});
	});
});

  <!-- Send custom events for clicks on Languages and Donate in header -->
  <script>
   (function() {
		var sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics = function(category, action, label, value) {
			try {
				if (typeof ga === 'function') {
					if (typeof ga.getAll === 'function') {
						var tracker = ga.getAll()[0];
						if (tracker) {
							if (typeof value != 'undefined') {
								tracker.send('event', category, action, label, value);
							} else {
								tracker.send('event', category, action, label);
							}
						}
					}
				}
			} catch (error) {
			}
		}
		var headerLanguageLinks = document.querySelectorAll('[data-lang]');
		if (headerLanguageLinks) {
			Array.prototype.forEach.call(headerLanguageLinks, function(el) {
				el.addEventListener('click', function() {
					sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
						'header', // category
						'click', // action
						'language' // label
					);
				});
			});
		}
		var headerDonateLink = document.querySelector('[data-header-donate]');
		if (headerDonateLink) {
			headerDonateLink.addEventListener('click', function() {
				sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
					'donate', // category
					'click', // action
					'header-donate' // label
				);
			});
		}
		var footerDonateLink = document.querySelector('[data-footer-donate]');
		if (footerDonateLink) {
			footerDonateLink.addEventListener('click', function() {
				sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
					'donate', // category
					'click', // action
					'footer-donate' // label
				);
			});
		}
		var teaserDonateLink = document.querySelector('[data-teaser-donate]');
		if (teaserDonateLink) {
			teaserDonateLink.addEventListener('click', function() {
				sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
					'donate', // category
					'click', // action
					'species-teaser' // label
				);
			});
		}
		var privacyPolicyLink = document.querySelector('#privacy-policy-link');
		if (privacyPolicyLink) {
			privacyPolicyLink.addEventListener('click', function() {
				sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
					'prefs', // category
					'click', // action
					'privacy-policy' // label
				);
				// console.log("Privacy Policy event logged.");
			});
		}
		var termsOfServiceLink = document.querySelector('#terms-of-service-link');
		if (termsOfServiceLink) {
			termsOfServiceLink.addEventListener('click', function() {
				sendCustomEventToGoogleAnalytics(
					'prefs', // category
					'click', // action
					'terms-of-service' // label
				);
				// console.log("Terms of Service event logged.");
			});
		}
	})();
  </script>
 </body>
</html>
